Highest Rated Marvel Razzie and lowest-rated MCU film =Closest to Daredevil film- Ant-Man and The Wasp :Quantumania- The review aggregator website Rotten Tomatoes reported an approval rating of 46% with an average rating of 5.5/10, based on 410 reviews. The site's critics consensus reads: "Ant-Man and the Wasp: Quantumania mostly lacks the spark of fun that elevated earlier adventures, but Jonathan Majors' Kang is a thrilling villain poised to alter the course of the MCU."  Closest to Inhumans- Secret Invasion- The review aggregator website Rotten Tomatoes reported an approval rating of 53%, with an average score of 6.1/10, based on 197 reviews. The site's critic's consensus states: "A well-deserved showcase for Samuel L. Jackson, Secret Invasion steadies itself after a somewhat slow start by taking the MCU in a darker, more mature direction."   The Marvel Razzies-1-Morbius-On Rotten Tomatoes, the film has an approval rating of 15% based on 283 reviews, with an average rating of 3.8/10. The website's critics consensus reads, "Cursed with uninspired effects, rote performances, and a borderline nonsensical story, this dreary mess is a vein [sic] attempt to make Morbius happen."[112] It ranks as the 16th worst-reviewed superhero movie on the site.  2-Daredevil film-On review aggregation website Rotten Tomatoes 43% of critics gave the film positive feedback, based on 228 reviews, with an average rating of 5.2/10. The critical consensus reads, "While Ben Affleck fits the role and the story is sporadically interesting, Daredevil is ultimately a dull, brooding origin story that fails to bring anything new to the genre."  3-Howard The Duck-Howard the Duck received mainly negative reviews from critics. On Rotten Tomatoes, the film has an approval rating of 13%, based on 83 reviews, with an average rating of 3.8/10, making it the lowest-rated Lucasfilm production. The site's consensus states: "While it has its moments, Howard the Duck suffers from an uneven tone and mediocre performances."   Worst of Marvel-Fant4stic-On the review aggregator website Rotten Tomatoes, 9% of 263 critics' reviews are positive, with an average rating of 3.6/10. The website's consensus reads: "Dull and downbeat, this Fantastic Four proves a woefully misguided attempt to translate a classic comic series without the humor, joy, or colorful thrills that made it great."[1] As of 2023, it the lowest-rated film on Rotten Tomatoes out of all theatrical films based on Marvel Comics properties.   The WORST of MCU-Inhumans-The review aggregator website Rotten Tomatoes reported an 11% approval rating, with an average rating of 3.70/10 based on 47 reviews. The website's consensus states, "Marvel's Inhumans sets a new low standard for the MCU with an unimaginative narrative, dull design work, weak characters, and disengaging soapy melodrama."Reviewing the season, Matt Liparota of Destructoid concluded, "Inhumans is a work with almost nothing of value for anyone. It's not even an interesting train wreck. It's just a boring, lifeless slog easily shooting to the top of the list of the worst things the MCU has produced in its near-decade of existence."   The DC Razzies- Catwoman-On Rotten Tomatoes, the film has an approval rating of 8% based on 197 reviews, with an average rating of 3.2/10. The site's critical consensus reads: "Halle Berry is the lone bright spot, but even she can't save this laughable action thriller".  BvS-On review aggregator website Rotten Tomatoes the film has an approval rating of 29% based on 439 reviews and an average rating of 5/10. Morbius: my review.  Morbius and his cousin Glorbius are living on a farm. Morbius is morbin' and Glorbius is glorbin'. Glorbius is a comic relief character. One time he says "They seee me glorbin', they hatin'" which everyone in the audience agrees is a joke. They live their happy lives. Until one day a man called Worbius appears and he says that the farm is in debt and if they don't pay 10 000 dollars by the end of the week it's going to be reposessed. Luckily there is a talent show in the valley and the main prize is 10 000 dollars. Morbius decides that they should do their morb and glorb routine, but his parents aren't happy about it. His father says that now he needs his help on the farm more than ever and Morbius has no time for talent shows. So Morbius is trying to work on the farm by day and still train his morbin' skills by night, but it is exhausting and he fails on both ends. So his father finds out and there is an emotional scene when he says "if morbin' is really what you want to do, then what kind of a father would I be if I stood in your way? Go on son. Get out of here and morb!" And so he does. For a while it looks like he's doing really well, his morbin' is improving and Glorbius' glorbin' is excellent. But alas Worbius finds out about it and decides to kill Glorbius to destroy his chances at winning. What you didn't know is that Worbius is worbin'. And he is very good at it. He wants to win the talent show and he won't let Morbius get in his way, and besides he really wants to get the farm. Morbius finds out about Glorbius' death and he seeks out Worbius. "You killed my cousin" - he cries. "No" - Worbius answers "I killed my own cousin. Who is also your cousin. For I am your cousin!"  They fight but Worbius escapes.  Morbius is wounded, but still he practices his morbin'. He really wants to win the talent show now.  The day finally comes. Morbius' friends Morbina and Quorbius are in the audience. Morbina is LGBT and Quorbius is ethnic. They don't have any character traits or story arcs, but at least they are in the movie so that's good.  There are some other talents, but finally the time comes for Worbius and his worbin' is exquisite. Morbius never knew that Worbius was this good at worbin'. He doubts himself. But he comes next so he mutters "It's morbin' time", which is the thing that people have heard in the memes. He start morbin', he's doing good, but he trips and falls and everybody's laughing. Worbius says "Give up, Morbius! You're nothing without Glorbius!" which he thinks will break his spirit, but it does the opposite. Morbius now remembers Glorbius and he gets up and starts morbin' and glorbin' AT THE SAME TIME. The audience is extatic, they have never seen anything like this. They award him the first place and give him 10 000 dollars. But then it turns out that an ancient curse is invoked and whichever cousin loses the talent show has to forefit his claims to the farm, so not only did Morbius win 10 000 dollars, but also the debt is absolved. Worbius has to work at the farm as a slave now, as is the custom. Morbius uses the money to throw a giant party for his friends and everyone in town. They are drinking, dancing and morbin'.  In the post credit scene we see a silhouette of a mysterious man zorbin'. It could be Zorbius, Morbius' uncle known from the comic. The screen fades to black and we see a text "MORBIUS WILL BE BACK IN MORBIUS 2: MORE MORBIN'"  All in all I think it was a good movie, great retelling of a classic tale. I would definitely like to see it and who knows, maybe one day I will.
